## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of population size P and time t. This is a fundamental problem in population ecology where various growth models describe how populations change depending on density-dependent and density-independent factors.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, Malthusian model)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth common in tumor/population modeling)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population threshold)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with flexible curvature)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (growth with constant removal rate)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized asymmetric growth model)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (density-dependent with hyperbolic saturation)
- Von Bertalanffy type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism-catabolism balance model)
- Time-dependent Malthusian: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (exponential growth with time-varying rate)
- Logistic with seasonal forcing: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (periodic environmental variation)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (higher-order density effects)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (fractional/anomalous growth dynamics)
- Delayed logistic approximation: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) + c2 * P * t (time-lagged density feedback approximation)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear proportionality to P (dP_dt ~ c*P) indicates density-independent exponential growth regime
- Quadratic term in P (c*P^2) indicates pairwise density-dependent interactions like competition or cooperation
- Product P*(1 - c*P) structure indicates logistic-type carrying capacity constraint where growth reverses sign at K
- Cubic terms in P (c*P^3) or triple products P*(P-a)*(K-P) indicate Allee effects with critical population thresholds
- Logarithmic dependence log(K/P) indicates Gompertz-type growth where per-capita rate declines logarithmically
- Ratio P/(1+c*P) indicates contest-type competition where resources are divided among individuals
- Sinusoidal time dependence sin(c*t) multiplied by growth terms indicates seasonal or periodic environmental forcing
- Fractional powers of P (P^c where 0<c<1) indicate surface-area-to-volume scaling effects in organism growth
- Additive constant terms independent of P indicate immigration/emigration or constant harvesting/stocking
- Exponential time factor exp(c*t) modulating growth rate indicates progressively changing environmental conditions

## Ground Truth Analysis

$$f(t, P) = 0.1404 \cdot (-1 + P/4.532) \cdot (1 - P/78.49) \cdot P + 0.1404 \cdot P / t^{4.532}$$

$$\alpha \cdot P^3 + \beta \cdot P^2 + \gamma \cdot P + \delta \cdot P/t^{4.532}$$

where:
- $\alpha = -0.1404/(4.532 \times 78.49) \approx -3.949 \times 10^{-4}$ (coefficient of $P^3$)
- $\beta = 0.1404 \cdot (1/78.49 + 1/4.532) \approx 0.1404 \cdot 0.2334 \approx 0.03277$ (coefficient of $P^2$)
- $\gamma = -0.1404$ (coefficient of $P$)
- $\delta = 0.1404$ (coefficient of $P \cdot t^{-4.532}$)

So GT = $a \cdot P^3 + b \cdot P^2 + c \cdot P + d \cdot P/t^e$ where $e \approx 4.532$.

The basis functions are: $P^3$, $P^2$, $P$, and $P/t^e$ (or equivalently $P \cdot t^{-e}$, where $e$ is a specific constant).

Now let me check each candidate:

### Candidate 1: $P^2 c_0 + P^2 c_1 + P c_2 + P c_3 t^{c_4}$
This simplifies to $(c_0+c_1)P^2 + c_2 P + c_3 P t^{c_4}$.
Missing $P^3$ term. Setting $c_4 = -4.532$ gives $P \cdot t^{-4.532}$, but no $P^3$.
**Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 2: $P^2 c_0 + P^2 c_1/t^2 + P c_2 + P c_3 t^{c_4} + P c_5 t^{c_6} \exp(P c_7)$
Has $\exp(P c_7)$ term - can set $c_7=0$ to make it constant, then $P c_5 t^{c_6}$ becomes another power of $t$ term. Also $P^2/t^2$ can't match $P^3$. Missing $P^3$.
If $c_7 = 0$: $P^2(c_0) + P^2 c_1/t^2 + Pc_2 + Pc_3 t^{c_4} + Pc_5 t^{c_6}$. Still no $P^3$ and has $P^2/t^2$.
**Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 3: $P^3 c_0 + P^2 c_1 + P c_2 + P c_3 + P c_4 t^{c_5} + P c_6$
Simplifies to $c_0 P^3 + c_1 P^2 + (c_2+c_3+c_6)P + c_4 P t^{c_5}$.
Setting $c_5 = -4.532$: $c_0 P^3 + c_1 P^2 + c' P + c_4 P/t^{4.532}$.
This matches the GT structure exactly!
**Candidate 3 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 4: $P^2 c_0 + P^2 c_1 + P c_2 + c_3 t^{c_4} + c_5 t^{c_6}$
The $t$-dependent terms are $c_3 t^{c_4} + c_5 t^{c_6}$, not multiplied by $P$. GT needs $P/t^{4.532}$. Missing $P^3$ and wrong $t$-dependence.
**Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 5: $P^2 c_0 + P c_1 + c_2 t^{c_3} + c_4 \exp(P^{c_5} c_6)$
Has $\exp$ term and $t$-terms not multiplied by $P$. Missing $P^3$. Can't match.
**Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 6: $P^2 c_0 + P c_1 + P^{c_2} c_3 + c_4 t^{c_5} + c_6/t^2$
$t$-dependent terms not multiplied by $P$. Missing $P^3$ (unless $c_2=3$, but then $P^{c_2}c_3 = c_3 P^3$ and we'd need $P/t^{4.532}$ which isn't available).
**Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 7: $P^2 c_0 + P c_1 + P c_2/t^5 + P c_3/(c_4+t)^5 + P c_5 \log(c_6 t+1)$
Missing $P^3$. Has $\log$ and rational $t$-functions instead of $P/t^{4.532}$.
**Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 8: Similar to 7 with extra $\exp$ term. Missing $P^3$.
**Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 9: $P^2 c_0 + P^2 c_1 + P^2 + P c_2 + P c_3 t^{c_4}$
Simplifies to $(c_0+c_1+1)P^2 + c_2 P + c_3 P t^{c_4}$. Missing $P^3$.
**Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 10: $P c_0 + P c_1 \exp(Pc_2) + c_3/t^5 + t^{c_4}$
$t$-terms not multiplied by $P$. Has $\exp$. Missing $P^3$.
**Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 11: $P^2 c_0 + P c_1 + P c_2 \exp(Pc_3) + c_4 t^{c_5} + c_6/t^5$
$t$-terms not multiplied by $P$. Has $\exp$.
**Candidate 11 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 12: Similar issues with $\exp$ and $t$-terms not multiplied by $P$.
**Candidate 12 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 13: $P^3 c_0 + P^2 c_1 + P^2 + P c_2 + P c_3 t^{c_4}$
Simplifies to $c_0 P^3 + (c_1+1)P^2 + c_2 P + c_3 P t^{c_4}$.
Setting $c_4 = -4.532$: matches GT structure!
**Candidate 13 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 14: $P^2 c_0 + P^2 c_1/t^2 + P c_2 + P c_3 t^{c_4} + P c_5 + P c_6 \log(c_7/(P+c_8)+1)$
Has $\log$ term and $P^2/t^2$. Missing $P^3$.
**Candidate 14 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 15: $P^3 c_0 + P^2 c_1 \log(c_2 t+1) + P c_3 + P^{c_4} c_5 t^{c_6} + c_7/t^5$
Has $\log$ in $P^2$ coefficient. The $t$-dependent term $c_7/t^5$ is not multiplied by $P$. Complex structure.
If $c_4=1$: $P^3 c_0 + P^2 c_1 \log(c_2 t+1) + Pc_3 + c_5 P t^{c_6} + c_7/t^5$. The $\log$ term can't be eliminated (it's multiplied by $P^2$, can't set $c_1=0$ without losing $P^2$ entirely). Actually we CAN set $c_1=0$, then: $c_0 P^3 + c_3 P + c_5 P t^{c_6} + c_7/t^5$. Missing $P^2$ and has $c_7/t^5$ (not $P/t^5$).
**Candidate 15 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 16: $P^3 c_0 + P^2 c_1 + P^2 c_2 + P^2 c_3 + P c_4 + P c_5 + P c_6 t^{c_7} + c_8/t^2$
Simplifies to $c_0 P^3 + (c_1+c_2+c_3)P^2 + (c_4+c_5)P + c_6 P t^{c_7} + c_8/t^2$.
The $c_8/t^2$ term is not multiplied by $P$. GT needs $P/t^{4.532}$, not $1/t^2$. Can't match.
**Candidate 16 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 17: $P^3 c_0 + P^2 c_1 + P^2 + P c_2 + P c_3 t^{c_4} + P c_5 \log(1+c_6/P)$
The $\log$ term: $P c_5 \log(1+c_6/P)$. For large $P$, this ≈ $c_5 c_6$, but it's not exactly a polynomial. Can we set $c_5=0$? Then: $c_0 P^3 + (c_1+1)P^2 + c_2 P + c_3 P t^{c_4}$. This matches GT!
**Candidate 17 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 18: $P^2 c_0 + P c_1 + P c_2/t^5 + P c_3/(c_4+t)^5 + P c_5/(Pc_6+1)$
Missing $P^3$. The $P/(Pc_6+1)$ term is not polynomial in $P$.
**Candidate 18 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 19: $Pc_0 + Pc_1 \exp(Pc_2) + c_3 t^{c_4} + c_5 t^{c_6} + c_7/t^5$
$t$-terms not multiplied by $P$. Has $\exp$.
**Candidate 19 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 20: $P^2 c_0 + P^2 c_1/t^2 + Pc_2 + Pc_3 + Pc_4 t^{c_5} + Pc_6 + P^{c_7}c_8$
If $c_7=3$: $c_8 P^3 + c_0 P^2 + c_1 P^2/t^2 + (c_2+c_3+c_6)P + c_4 P t^{c_5}$. Has $P^2/t^2$ which can't be eliminated (unless $c_1=0$). If $c_1=0$: $c_8 P^3 + c_0 P^2 + c'P + c_4 P t^{c_5}$. Setting $c_5=-4.532$: matches!
**Candidate 20 verdict: [MATCH]**

### Candidate 21: $P^2 c_0 + P^2 + Pc_1 + Pc_2 t^{c_3}$

### Candidate 24: $P^3 c_0 + Pc_1 + Pc_2/(P+1) + c_3 t^{c_4} + c_5 t^{c_6}$

### Candidate 27: $P^2 c_0 + P^2 c_1 + Pc_2 + Pc_3 + Pc_4 t^{c_5} + Pc_6$

### Candidate 32: $P^2 c_0 + P^2 c_1 + Pc_2 + Pc_3 \exp(c_4 t) + c_5 t^{c_6}$

$= c_0 P^3 + c_1 P^2 + (c_2+1)P + c_3 P t^{c_4}$. Setting $c_4=-4.532$: matches!
